UN_V2_MATHIAS_PROFILE Matia is a warrior of the the Gluttony Layer and one of the first citizens of Sephira. She takes the side of those unable to defend themselves, both out of compassion, and out of a desire to fight stronger opponents. She lets her blade do the talking, choosing to live her life on the battlefield. She is so fond of battle that many have taken to calling her blood-crazed.

UN_V2_GL_LACHESIS_PROFILE Lachesis is the second of Soren's creations after Atropos, possessing a humanoid form closer to that of a teenager. Bestowed with the ability to control and manipulate organic matter, Lachesis revels in the gift of life, following Soren around the world to heal sickness and disease. Her curiosity and compassion for humans knows no bounds. Lachesis waits patiently for the day she can explore this wonderful world once more with her master, and bring an age of happiness to all.
